This creamery was pretty busy with an after lunch rush on Saturday, that being said after ordering my friends and I got our ice cream about half an hour later. Granted the ice cream is made/ prepared to order and the presentation, taste, and texture was nice. It's an interesting idea but to play around with an industry that typically has fast food timing when it comes to the end result the wait doesn't seem to justify the product. I also happened to choose two flavors on their menu that weren't available so I went with my third option, a take on strawberries and cream, The Owen Experiment.</Text>

As someone who can't consume dairy and has a tree nut allergy, the staff at Atomic Creamery went above and beyond with their product and my order! Never have I had such creamy, unique flavors in a non-dairy ice cream! I highly recommend the strawberry, and even my dairy eating friends complimented how similar the taste was to real ice cream. Their nationwide delivery was a breeze and I will be ordering again soon! Thank you!<//review>

< Review>
i was a little disappointed by this ice cream spot after reading the reviews about exotic flavors. most flavors are generic- chocolate varieties, cheesecake of some sort, vanillas, your typical ice cream flavors which were just ok. they had four exotic flavors consisting of rosewater when i visited- which were great (only because i love flowery tasting ice cream in general) i got the orange blossom ice cream (a flowery ice cream not fruity) which was better in a mashti sandwich. my bf got the rosewater saffron which was also good. however, for the drive and destination location, i can't say their flowery ice cream (nor their normal flavors) even compares to some other i've had at ici, bi-rite or even carmela's. it's also on the pricey side given atmosphere and portions. i wouldn't go back given the other choices in the city.< /Review>

3</Rate>
< review>
Walked in 1st visit. Small frontage order area, register to the right small bit of counter seating to the left. Kind of like a Creamisry with fresher ingredients. The concept is to use top notch ingredients and create ice cream using the nitrogen process. It's an old chemistry class trick that when done right using their custom machines, makes very smooth ice cream. Ok, regarding the smoothness, straight up I'd be back in a heartbeat for the product. As for price the website looks like no update since March 2018 (?) We were able to order the Lil Bites (?) maybe used to be Lil Scientists. This is a limited menu of smaller sized, but less expensive choices @ 4.50$/ea. This choice was a value and as a dinner dessert plenty for portion size. A few downsides... We ordered thinking we were first to be served. With only two ice cream machines in use, there were actually two orders ahead of us. We didn't want to seem impatient, but our order was ready 20+ minutes after ring up. Be cautious if you are going to a movie, etc. There was what looked like three young staff and one Supervisor/Mgr on shift to make orders. With orders coming in I did not see the machine bowls filled, churning out ice cream. I have no clue what wait time is when they have a rush but I'm sure it's more than 20+ minutes. There was the usual pop music medium volume in the store. Hip n cool, yes, but bummer the staff was shouting over the combo of music and the air blasts the nitrogen made as it hit the mixing bowl. I didn't care to much for one employee discussing work hours and employee habits while making the ice cream. As first time customers, I thought the register/counter person could have been more helpful or friendly to us. The girl at the "finishing" station was moving a bit slow compared to back service restuarant people I've worked with. Again as commented only one machine of two was used on average, sometimes two. Magically, they did get orders out in a roughly smooth operation. There was a looseness to the group for example a woman came in and just waited at the register for service for quite some time before being noticed. The place was very clean as expected. A little bit of old ice cream and toppings floating in the dipper wells. I did notice an employee rinsing blades in the dipper wells instead of being sanitized in the sink. Overall an average experience with very good ice cream. I can see this is a good product by people with good intentions. FYI, I've managed and sold ice cream, not easy. My intent here is not to anonymously rip on a store. I hope they resolve the output issue to make more product faster but still keep quality. Also, I know it's a challenge to manage kids getting minimum wage, but they owe the company to represent the product and encourage people to come back. Leasing at Fashion Island is not cheap. Oh and its AUG 2018, keeping websites current is extra work on top of 14 hour days, I know I've worked them. But current info sells the awesome fresh ingredient model to a wider group of people for you... Thank you kindly for the great ice cream tonight.<//review>

While not necessarily a big deal if you have time, it gets annoying and ultimately ruins the entire purpose of a speedy drive thru experience. < review>
Taken from my Yelp review written on June 26, 2017.
Came here on a hot, Sunday afternoon at around 16:45 (4:45pm) with my friend here on the drive thru. I ordered 6 McDoubles, 6 Mcchickens, and 2 Large Dr. Peppers which was almost $26.
After driving through, I did not realize they had 2 windows. Lucky for me, I came on a slow day so I was able to reverse. I gave my card to the person and then she gave it back to me. I did not know whether to go to the second window or not so I just drove back to the other window. I was staring at the window waiting for someone. No one came until about 5-7 minutes later after chatting with my friend over him being grumpy (yes he was hungry). Anyways, I got my food and then was greet with a generic "thank you, have a nice day."
The food was good though probably because I had to wait. I liked the fact that I had to wait for it because usually it means that they are giving fresh new meat rather than something that is sitting there (a practice that some fast food managers like to do in order to save some precious stock inventory money). My only complaint is the service I get at this location. I have been here a few other times on the drive through, but never have once I seen an employee being happy working here. Two things I wanted to mention on that regard.
First, when i backed out, the lady gave me a look. Did not smile and just took my card. She did not even say a word which led me to think that she probably wanted to either laugh at my mistake or just think that I was an idiot. She would not say anything after one silly mistake.
Second, at the second drive thru window, no one greeted me. The drinks weren't even given to us as we were thirsty on a nice hot day until our orders were ready. I used to work at a fast food and I remember drinks were given first before the orders. I would tell them that it would come out in a moment or an indication that we will be waiting longer than usual. (5 minutes is usually the standard time for waiting for our food). I wonder if my order was way too big but I felt that the service could have been improved.
Finally as I mentioned earlier, there was no communication of when is my order ready or if I needed any sauce. There was not even a single greeting acknowledging that I was here at all which I feel is standard for all the McDonalds I have been.
Overall though, compared to several Mcdonalds I have gone in the past, this is probably one of the most depressing one's I've been to on the drive thru side. The service here is okay and can be improved. I was the only car at that time. While I do not mind the wait, there should clearly be some indication that I would wait or at least do a friendly greeting where I am appreciated by visiting this location. The only reason why I am not giving a one star is because the burgers were actually fresh. However, I am disappointed in the service at this location.<//review>
